remarks:
remarks:        - Communities accepted from peering members -
remarks:        We accept traditional, extended, and large BGP communities
remarks:        For extended BGP communities simply prepend the communities with rt
remarks:        Example: (rt:65000:ASN)
remarks:        For large BGP communities simply prepend the communities with 9033
remarks:        Example: (9033:65000:ASN)
remarks:
remarks:        (65000:ASN) do not announce this route to ASN
remarks:        (65000:0) do not announce this route to any ASN
remarks:        (64960:ASN) do announce this route to ASN if (65000:0) is set
remarks:
remarks:        (65001:0) prepend peer AS 1 time to all
remarks:        (65001:ASN) prepend peer AS 1 time to ASN
remarks:        (65002:0) prepend peer AS 2 times to all
remarks:        (65002:ASN) prepend peer AS 2 times to ASN
remarks:        (65003:0) prepend peer AS 3 times to all
remarks:        (65003:ASN) prepend peer AS 3 times to ASN
remarks:
remarks:        (65050:0) do not announce this route to local peers
remarks:        (65050:1) do not announce this route to remote peers
remarks:        (65070:0) do not announce this route to any METRO_ID
remarks:        (65070:METRO_ID) do not announce this route to METRO_ID
remarks:        (64970:METRO_ID) do announce this route to METRO_ID if (65070:0) is set
remarks:
remarks:        In addition to our own communities we also support the EURO-IX large BGP communities
remarks:        refer to https://www.euro-ix.net/en/forixps/large-bgp-communities/ for more information
remarks:
remarks:        (9033:0:ASN) do not announce this route to ASN
remarks:        (9033:0:0) do not announce this route to any ASN
remarks:        (9033:1:ASN) do announce this route to ASN if (9033:0:0) is set
remarks:
remarks:        (9033:101:0) prepend peer AS 1 time to all
remarks:        (9033:101:ASN) prepend peer AS 1 time to ASN
remarks:        (9033:102:0) prepend peer AS 2 times to all
remarks:        (9033:102:ASN) prepend peer AS 2 times to ASN
remarks:        (9033:103:0) prepend peer AS 3 times to all
remarks:        (9033:103:ASN) prepend peer AS 3 times to ASN
remarks:
remarks:        (9033:900:0) do not announce this route to local peers
remarks:        (9033:900:1) do not announce this route to remote peers
remarks:        (9033:910:0) do not announce this route to any METRO_ID
remarks:        (9033:910:METRO_ID) do not announce this route to METRO_ID
remarks:        (9033:911:METRO_ID) do announce this route to METRO_ID if (9033:910:0) is set
remarks:
remarks:        - Communities advertised by the route servers -
remarks:        Our route servers will also tag informational communities to each exported route
remarks:        These communities are meant to help our peers apply proper filtering
remarks:
remarks:        (65040:0) This route comes from a local peer
remarks:        (65040:1) This route comes from a remote peer
remarks:        (65060:METRO_ID) This route comes from a peer in METRO_ID
remarks:        (9033:1900:0) This route comes from a local peer
remarks:        (9033:1900:1) This route comes from a remote peer
remarks:        (9033:1903:METRO_ID) This route comes from a peer in METRO_ID
remarks:
remarks:        METRO_ID list: https://docs.megaport.com/ix/metro-ids/
remarks:        Please visit our looking glass at https://lg.megaport.com/
